+    <script>
+      const qs = (id) => document.getElementById(id);
+      const $ = (selector, root = document) => root.querySelector(selector);
+      const $$ = (selector, root = document) => Array.from(root.querySelectorAll(selector));
+
+      const state = {
+        useMock: false,
+        mergeMock: false,
+        showTrace: true,
+        healthProfile: null,
+      };
+
+      const setBusy = (btn, busy) => {
+        btn.disabled = busy;
+        btn.textContent = busy ? "请求中..." : btn.dataset.label;
+      };
+
+      const pretty = (data) => JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
+
+      const safeJson = async (response) => {
+        const text = await response.text();
+        try {
+          return JSON.parse(text);
+        } catch (err) {
+          return { raw: text };
+        }
+      };
+
+      const toastResult = (el, payload) => {
+        el.textContent = pretty(payload);
+      };
+
+      const scenarioMeta = [
+        { name: "通勤", hint: "雨天风大时建议提前出门", risk: "medium" },
+        { name: "运动", hint: "空气质量 < 100 更适合跑步", risk: "low" },
+        { name: "洗车", hint: "未来 12 小时无降水最佳", risk: "low" },
+        { name: "出行", hint: "关注目的地温差与降雨", risk: "medium" },
+        { name: "风湿", hint: "湿冷天气注意关节保暖", risk: "medium" },
+        { name: "哮喘", hint: "AQI 偏高减少户外强度", risk: "high" },
+        { name: "光敏", hint: "UV>7 需加强防晒", risk: "medium" },
+        { name: "高温", hint: "体感温度极端需减少曝晒", risk: "high" },
+      ];
+
+      const renderScenes = () => {
+        const grid = qs("sceneGrid");

+            <p class="${item.risk === "high" ? "risk-high" : ""}">${item.hint}</p>
+            <span class="tag">${item.risk}</span>
+          `;
+          grid.appendChild(div);
+        });
+      };
+

+          ts: "2026-03-16T06:50:00+08:00",

+          source: "mock",

+          task_id: 1024,
+          status: "scheduled",
+          nextRun: "2026-03-16T06:30:00+08:00",
+          channel: "push",
+          source: "mock",
+        }),
+        memory: () => [
+          { role: "user", content: "最近总是腿部酸痛", timestamp: "2026-03-15T20:18:00+00:00" },
+          { role: "assistant", content: "已记录健康偏好，将关注湿冷天气提醒。", timestamp: "2026-03-15T20:18:10+00:00" },
+        ],
+        rag: () => [
+          { id: "health_rheumatism", title: "湿冷与关节不适", tags: ["health"], score: 0.82 },
+          { id: "commute_rain", title: "雨天通勤安全提示", tags: ["commute"], score: 0.71 },
+        ],
+      };
+
+      const updateModeIndicator = () => {
+        const el = qs("modeIndicator");
+        if (state.useMock) {
+          el.textContent = "Mock: 仅使用模拟数据";
+        } else if (state.mergeMock) {
+          el.textContent = "Hybrid: 后端失败自动回退";
+        } else {
+          el.textContent = "Auto: 后端优先";
+        }
+      };
+
+      const setPillActive = (group) => {
+        $$(".pill", group).forEach((pill) => {
+          const input = $("input", pill);
+          pill.classList.toggle("active", input.checked);
+        });
+      };
+
+      const bindPills = (groupId) => {
+        const group = qs(groupId);
+        if (!group) return;
+        group.addEventListener("change", () => setPillActive(group));
+        setPillActive(group);
+      };
+
+      const mergeTrace = (data) => {
+        if (!state.showTrace) {
+          if (data && typeof data === "object") {
+            const copy = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));
+            delete copy.traceId;
+            return copy;
+          }
+        }
+        return data;
+      };
+
+      const updateDecisionStats = (data) => {
+        const target = qs("decisionStats");
+        if (!data) return;
+        const items = [
+          { label: "Intent", value: data.intent || "--" },
+          { label: "Risk", value: data.decision?.riskLevel || "--" },
+          { label: "Comfort", value: data.environment?.comfortIndex ?? "--" },
+          { label: "Health", value: data.healthRiskLevel || "--" },
+        ];
+        target.innerHTML = "";
+        items.forEach((item) => {
+          const div = document.createElement("div");
+          div.className = "stat";
+          div.innerHTML = `${item.label}<strong>${item.value}</strong>`;
+          target.appendChild(div);
+        });
+      };
+
+      const updateHealthSummary = (profile, alerts = []) => {
+        const target = qs("healthSummary");
+        target.innerHTML = "";
+        if (!profile) {
+          target.innerHTML = `<div class="health-card"><h4>尚未建立档案</h4><p>保存健康档案后可生成个性化提醒。</p></div>`;
+          return;
+        }
+        const card = document.createElement("div");
+        card.className = "health-card";
+        card.innerHTML = `<h4>健康档案</h4><p>条件：${profile.conditions.join(", ") || "无"}<br/>敏感备注：${profile.note || "无"}</p>`;
+        target.appendChild(card);
+        if (alerts.length) {
+          alerts.forEach((alert) => {
+            const c = document.createElement("div");
+            c.className = "health-card";
+            c.innerHTML = `<h4>${alert.condition}</h4><p>${alert.actions.join("，")}</p>`;
+            target.appendChild(c);
+          });
+        } else {
+          const empty = document.createElement("div");
+          empty.className = "health-card";
+          empty.innerHTML = `<h4>暂无提醒</h4><p>当前环境未触发健康风险。</p>`;
+          target.appendChild(empty);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callWithFallback = async (fn, fallback) => {
+        if (state.useMock) return fallback();
+        try {
+          return await fn();
+        } catch (err) {
+          if (state.mergeMock) {
+            return fallback();
+          }
+          throw err;
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callQuery = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockQueryBtn" : "queryBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const payload = { query: qs("queryText").value.trim() };
+        const sessionId = qs("querySession").value.trim();
+        const city = qs("queryCity").value.trim();
+        const adcode = qs("queryAdcode").value.trim();
+        const time = qs("queryTime").value.trim();
+        const scenario = $("input[name='scenario']:checked")?.value;
+        if (sessionId) payload.sessionId = sessionId;
+        if (city) payload.city = city;
+        if (adcode) payload.adcode = adcode;
+        if (time) payload.time = time;
+        if (scenario) payload.scenario = scenario;
+
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch("/api/v1/query", {
+            method: "POST",
+            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
+            body: JSON.stringify(payload),
+          });
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.query() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.query);
+          updateDecisionStats(data);
+          updateHealthSummary(state.healthProfile, data.healthAlerts || []);
+          toastResult(qs("queryResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+          if (data.evidence) renderRagTable(data.evidence);
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("queryResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callWeather = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockWeatherBtn" : "weatherBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        const city = qs("weatherCity").value.trim();
+        const adcode = qs("weatherAdcode").value.trim();
+        const lang = qs("weatherLang").value;
+        if (city) params.set("city", city);
+        if (adcode) params.set("adcode", adcode);
+        params.set("lang", lang);
+        ["extended", "forecast", "hourly", "minutely", "indices"].forEach((key) => {
+          if (qs(key).checked) params.set(key, "true");
+        });
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/misc/weather?${params.toString()}`);
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.weather() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.weather);
+          toastResult(qs("weatherResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("weatherResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callMemory = async (action, forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(action === "fetch" ? "memoryFetchBtn" : "memoryClearBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const sessionId = qs("memorySession").value.trim();
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/memory/${sessionId}`, {
+            method: action === "fetch" ? "GET" : "DELETE",
+          });
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.memory() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.memory);
+          toastResult(qs("memoryResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("memoryResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callForecast = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockForecastBtn" : "forecastBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        params.set("lat", qs("forecastLat").value.trim());
+        params.set("lon", qs("forecastLon").value.trim());
+        params.set("hours", qs("forecastHours").value.trim());
+        params.set("days", qs("forecastDays").value.trim());
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/forecast?${params.toString()}`);
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.forecast() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.forecast);
+          toastResult(qs("forecastResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("forecastResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callAqi = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockAqiBtn" : "aqiBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        params.set("lat", qs("aqiLat").value.trim());
+        params.set("lon", qs("aqiLon").value.trim());
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/aqi?${params.toString()}`);
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.aqi() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.aqi);
+          toastResult(qs("aqiResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("aqiResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callTask = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockTaskBtn" : "taskBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        let metadata = {};
+        try {
+          metadata = JSON.parse(qs("taskMeta").value || "{}");
+        } catch (err) {
+          metadata = { raw: qs("taskMeta").value };
+        }
+        const payload = {
+          type: qs("taskType").value,
+          scheduled_time: qs("taskTime").value.trim(),
+          priority: Number(qs("taskPriority").value || 5),
+          metadata,
+        };
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch("/api/v1/tasks", {
+            method: "POST",
+            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
+            body: JSON.stringify(payload),
+          });
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.task() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.task);
+          toastResult(qs("taskResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("taskResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const renderRagTable = (items) => {
+        const body = qs("ragTable").querySelector("tbody");
+        body.innerHTML = "";
+        (items || []).forEach((item) => {
+          const row = document.createElement("tr");
+          row.innerHTML = `
+            <td>${item.title || item.id}</td>
+            <td>${(item.tags || []).join(", ")}</td>
+            <td>${item.score ?? "--"}</td>
+          `;
+          body.appendChild(row);
+        });
+      };
+
+      const callRag = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockRagBtn" : "ragBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.rag() : await callWithFallback(() => Promise.resolve(mock.rag()), mock.rag);
+          renderRagTable(data);
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const saveProfile = () => {
+        const conditions = $$("#conditionPills input:checked").map((input) => input.value);
+        const profile = {
+          user_id: qs("healthUser").value.trim(),
+          conditions,
+          note: qs("healthNote").value.trim(),
+          consent: true,
+          updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
+        };
+        state.healthProfile = profile;
+        updateHealthSummary(profile, []);
+        toastResult(qs("healthResult"), profile);
+      };
+
+      const clearProfile = () => {
+        state.healthProfile = null;
+        updateHealthSummary(null, []);
+        toastResult(qs("healthResult"), { status: "deleted" });
+      };
+
+      const init = () => {
+        bindPills("scenarioPills");
+        bindPills("conditionPills");
+        renderScenes();
+        updateHealthSummary(null, []);
+        updateModeIndicator();
+      };
+
+      qs("queryBtn").dataset.label = "发送决策";
+      qs("mockQueryBtn").dataset.label = "示例响应";
+      qs("weatherBtn").dataset.label = "查询";
+      qs("mockWeatherBtn").dataset.label = "模拟天气";
+      qs("memoryFetchBtn").dataset.label = "读取记忆";
+      qs("memoryClearBtn").dataset.label = "清理记忆";
+      qs("forecastBtn").dataset.label = "获取预报";
+      qs("mockForecastBtn").dataset.label = "模拟预报";
+      qs("aqiBtn").dataset.label = "获取 AQI";
+      qs("mockAqiBtn").dataset.label = "模拟 AQI";
+      qs("taskBtn").dataset.label = "创建任务";
+      qs("mockTaskBtn").dataset.label = "模拟任务";
+      qs("ragBtn").dataset.label = "获取证据";
+      qs("mockRagBtn").dataset.label = "模拟证据";
+      qs("saveProfileBtn").dataset.label = "保存档案";
+      qs("clearProfileBtn").dataset.label = "删除档案";
+
+      qs("queryBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callQuery(false));
+      qs("mockQueryBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callQuery(true));
+      qs("weatherBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callWeather(false));
+      qs("mockWeatherBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callWeather(true));
+      qs("memoryFetchBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callMemory("fetch", false));
+      qs("memoryClearBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callMemory("clear", false));
+      qs("forecastBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callForecast(false));
+      qs("mockForecastBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callForecast(true));
+      qs("aqiBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callAqi(false));
+      qs("mockAqiBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callAqi(true));
+      qs("taskBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callTask(false));
+      qs("mockTaskBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callTask(true));
+      qs("ragBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callRag(false));
+      qs("mockRagBtn").addEventListener("click", () => callRag(true));
+      qs("saveProfileBtn").addEventListener("click", saveProfile);
+      qs("clearProfileBtn").addEventListener("click", clearProfile);
+
+      qs("mockToggle").addEventListener("change", (event) => {
+        state.useMock = event.target.checked;
+        if (state.useMock) {
+          state.mergeMock = false;
+          qs("mergeMockToggle").checked = false;
+        }
+        updateModeIndicator();
+      });
+
+      qs("mergeMockToggle").addEventListener("change", (event) => {
+        state.mergeMock = event.target.checked;
+        if (state.mergeMock) {
+          state.useMock = false;
+          qs("mockToggle").checked = false;
+        }
+        updateModeIndicator();
+      });
+
+      qs("showTraceToggle").addEventListener("change", (event) => {
+        state.showTrace = event.target.checked;
+      });
+
+      init();
+    </script>
+  </body>
+</html>
*** End Patch

+        ],
+        rag: () => [
+          { id: "health_rheumatism", title: "湿冷与关节不适", tags: ["health"], score: 0.82 },
+          { id: "commute_rain", title: "雨天通勤安全提示", tags: ["commute"], score: 0.71 },
+        ],
+      };
+
+      const updateModeIndicator = () => {
+        const el = qs("modeIndicator");
+        if (state.useMock) {
+          el.textContent = "Mock: 仅使用模拟数据";
+        } else if (state.mergeMock) {
+          el.textContent = "Hybrid: 后端失败自动回退";
+        } else {
+          el.textContent = "Auto: 后端优先";
+        }
+      };
+
+      const setPillActive = (group) => {
+        $$(".pill", group).forEach((pill) => {
+          const input = $("input", pill);
+          pill.classList.toggle("active", input.checked);
+        });
+      };
+
+      const bindPills = (groupId) => {
+        const group = qs(groupId);
+        if (!group) return;
+        group.addEventListener("change", () => setPillActive(group));
+        setPillActive(group);
+      };
+
+      const mergeTrace = (data) => {
+        if (!state.showTrace) {
+          if (data && typeof data === "object") {
+            const copy = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));
+            delete copy.traceId;
+            return copy;
+          }
+        }
+        return data;
+      };
+
+      const updateDecisionStats = (data) => {
+        const target = qs("decisionStats");
+        if (!data) return;
+        const items = [
+          { label: "Intent", value: data.intent || "--" },
+          { label: "Risk", value: data.decision?.riskLevel || "--" },
+          { label: "Comfort", value: data.environment?.comfortIndex ?? "--" },
+          { label: "Health", value: data.healthRiskLevel || "--" },
+        ];
+        target.innerHTML = "";
+        items.forEach((item) => {
+          const div = document.createElement("div");
+          div.className = "stat";
+          div.innerHTML = `${item.label}<strong>${item.value}</strong>`;
+          target.appendChild(div);
+        });
+      };
+
+      const updateHealthSummary = (profile, alerts = []) => {
+        const target = qs("healthSummary");
+        target.innerHTML = "";
+        if (!profile) {
+          target.innerHTML = `<div class="health-card"><h4>尚未建立档案</h4><p>保存健康档案后可生成个性化提醒。</p></div>`;
+          return;
+        }
+        const card = document.createElement("div");
+        card.className = "health-card";
+        card.innerHTML = `<h4>健康档案</h4><p>条件：${profile.conditions.join(", ") || "无"}<br/>敏感备注：${profile.note || "无"}</p>`;
+        target.appendChild(card);
+        if (alerts.length) {
+          alerts.forEach((alert) => {
+            const c = document.createElement("div");
+            c.className = "health-card";
+            c.innerHTML = `<h4>${alert.condition}</h4><p>${alert.actions.join("，")}</p>`;
+            target.appendChild(c);
+          });
+        } else {
+          const empty = document.createElement("div");
+          empty.className = "health-card";
+          empty.innerHTML = `<h4>暂无提醒</h4><p>当前环境未触发健康风险。</p>`;
+          target.appendChild(empty);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callWithFallback = async (fn, fallback) => {
+        if (state.useMock) return fallback();
+        try {
+          return await fn();
+        } catch (err) {
+          if (state.mergeMock) {
+            return fallback();
+          }
+          throw err;
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callQuery = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockQueryBtn" : "queryBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const payload = { query: qs("queryText").value.trim() };
+        const sessionId = qs("querySession").value.trim();
+        const city = qs("queryCity").value.trim();
+        const adcode = qs("queryAdcode").value.trim();
+        const time = qs("queryTime").value.trim();
+        const scenario = $("input[name='scenario']:checked")?.value;
+        if (sessionId) payload.sessionId = sessionId;
+        if (city) payload.city = city;
+        if (adcode) payload.adcode = adcode;
+        if (time) payload.time = time;
+        if (scenario) payload.scenario = scenario;
+
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch("/api/v1/query", {
+            method: "POST",
+            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
+            body: JSON.stringify(payload),
+          });
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.query() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.query);
+          updateDecisionStats(data);
+          updateHealthSummary(state.healthProfile, data.healthAlerts || []);
+          toastResult(qs("queryResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+          if (data.evidence) renderRagTable(data.evidence);
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("queryResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callWeather = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockWeatherBtn" : "weatherBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        const city = qs("weatherCity").value.trim();
+        const adcode = qs("weatherAdcode").value.trim();
+        const lang = qs("weatherLang").value;
+        if (city) params.set("city", city);
+        if (adcode) params.set("adcode", adcode);
+        params.set("lang", lang);
+        ["extended", "forecast", "hourly", "minutely", "indices"].forEach((key) => {
+          if (qs(key).checked) params.set(key, "true");
+        });
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/misc/weather?${params.toString()}`);
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.weather() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.weather);
+          toastResult(qs("weatherResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("weatherResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callMemory = async (action, forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(action === "fetch" ? "memoryFetchBtn" : "memoryClearBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const sessionId = qs("memorySession").value.trim();
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/memory/${sessionId}`, {
+            method: action === "fetch" ? "GET" : "DELETE",
+          });
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.memory() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.memory);
+          toastResult(qs("memoryResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("memoryResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callForecast = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockForecastBtn" : "forecastBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        params.set("lat", qs("forecastLat").value.trim());
+        params.set("lon", qs("forecastLon").value.trim());
+        params.set("hours", qs("forecastHours").value.trim());
+        params.set("days", qs("forecastDays").value.trim());
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/forecast?${params.toString()}`);
+          return await safeJson(response);
+        };
+        try {
+          const data = forceMock ? mock.forecast() : await callWithFallback(runRequest, mock.forecast);
+          toastResult(qs("forecastResult"), mergeTrace(data));
+        } catch (err) {
+          toastResult(qs("forecastResult"), { error: String(err) });
+        } finally {
+          setBusy(btn, false);
+        }
+      };
+
+      const callAqi = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockAqiBtn" : "aqiBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        const params = new URLSearchParams();
+        params.set("lat", qs("aqiLat").value.trim());
+        params.set("lon", qs("aqiLon").value.trim());
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/aqi?${params.toString()}`);

+      const callTask = async (forceMock = false) => {
+        const btn = qs(forceMock ? "mockTaskBtn" : "taskBtn");
+        setBusy(btn, true);
+        let metadata = {};
+        try {
+          metadata = JSON.parse(qs("taskMeta").value || "{}");
+        } catch (err) {
+          metadata = { raw: qs("taskMeta").value };

+          type: qs("taskType").value,
+          scheduled_time: qs("taskTime").value.trim(),
+          priority: Number(qs("taskPriority").value || 5),
+          metadata,
+        };
+        const runRequest = async () => {
+          const response = await fetch("/api/v1/tasks", {

       const animatePulse = () => {
         const pulse = qs("wallPulse");
         if (!pulse) return;
         let value = 78;
         setInterval(() => {
           value += Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
           value = Math.max(60, Math.min(92, value));
           pulse.textContent = `${value}%`;
         }, 1800);
       };
 
       animatePulse();
+
+      const drawLineChart = (canvasId, points, color) => {
+        const canvas = qs(canvasId);
+        if (!canvas) return;
+        const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
+        const w = canvas.width;
+        const h = canvas.height;
+        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
+        ctx.strokeStyle = color;
+        ctx.lineWidth = 2;
+        ctx.beginPath();
+        points.forEach((p, idx) => {
+          const x = (w / (points.length - 1)) * idx;
+          const y = h - p * h;
+          if (idx === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);
+          else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
+        });
+        ctx.stroke();
+        ctx.fillStyle = color;
+        points.forEach((p, idx) => {
+          const x = (w / (points.length - 1)) * idx;
+          const y = h - p * h;
+          ctx.beginPath();
+          ctx.arc(x, y, 2.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
+          ctx.fill();
+        });
+      };
+
+      const updateGauge = (value) => {
+        const arc = qs("aqiGaugeArc");
+        const label = qs("aqiGaugeValue");
+        if (!arc || !label) return;
+        const clamped = Math.max(0, Math.min(200, value));
+        const ratio = clamped / 200;
+        const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * 46;
+        const dash = circumference * ratio;
+        arc.setAttribute("stroke-dasharray", `${dash} ${circumference - dash}`);
+        label.textContent = clamped;
+      };
+
+      const animateCharts = () => {
+        const rain = [0.2, 0.35, 0.6, 0.55, 0.4, 0.3, 0.2];
+        const traffic = [0.7, 0.65, 0.6, 0.5, 0.52, 0.48, 0.45];
+        drawLineChart("rainChart", rain, "rgba(34,211,238,0.9)");
+        drawLineChart("trafficChart", traffic, "rgba(245,158,11,0.9)");
+        setInterval(() => {
+          rain.push(Math.max(0.1, Math.min(0.9, rain.shift() + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2)));
+          traffic.push(Math.max(0.2, Math.min(0.9, traffic.shift() + (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2)));
+          drawLineChart("rainChart", rain, "rgba(34,211,238,0.9)");
+          drawLineChart("trafficChart", traffic, "rgba(245,158,11,0.9)");
+        }, 2500);
+      };
+
+      animateCharts();
*** End Patch

       const toastResult = (el, payload) => {

+      const addCapEvent = (service, status, detail = "") => {
+        const timeline = qs("capTimeline");
+        if (!timeline) return;
+        const item = document.createElement("div");
+        item.className = "cap-event";
+        const now = new Date().toLocaleTimeString("zh-CN", { hour12: false });
+        item.innerHTML = `<strong>${now}</strong> [${service}] ${status}${detail ? ` · ${detail}` : ""}`;
+        timeline.prepend(item);
+        while (timeline.children.length > 24) timeline.removeChild(timeline.lastChild);
+        state.calls += 1;
+        const counter = qs("capCounter");
+        if (counter) counter.textContent = `${state.calls} 次`;
+      };
+
+      const setServiceTag = (key, label, isOk = true) => {
+        if (key === "api") {
+          const tag = qs("capApiTag");
+          if (!tag) return;
+          tag.textContent = `API ${label}`;
+          tag.style.borderColor = isOk ? "rgba(82,196,26,0.55)" : "rgba(255,77,79,0.55)";
+          tag.style.color = isOk ? "var(--ink)" : "#ffd8d9";

+          tag.style.borderColor = isOk ? "rgba(82,196,26,0.55)" : "rgba(255,77,79,0.55)";
+          tag.style.color = isOk ? "var(--ink)" : "#ffd8d9";
+        }
+      };
